{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="134" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="141" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}" class="Module">plfa.part2.Subtyping</a> <a id="162" class="Keyword">where</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
This chapter introduces *subtyping*, a concept that plays an important
role in object-oriented languages. Subtyping enables code to be more
reusable by allowing it to work on objects of many different
types. Thus, subtyping provides a kind of polymorphism. In general, a
type `A` can be a subtype of another type `B`, written `A <: B`, when
an object of type `A` has all the capabilities expected of something
of type `B`. Or put another way, a type `A` can be a subtype of type
`B` when it is safe to substitute something of type `A` into code that
expects something of type `B`.  This is know as the *Liskov
Substitution Principle*. Given this semantic meaning of subtyping, a
subtype relation should always be reflexive and transitive. When
`A` is a subtype of `B`, that is, `A <: B`, we may also refer to
`B` as a supertype of `A`.

To formulate a type system for a language with subtyping, one simply
adds the *subsumption rule*, which states that a term of type `A`
can also have type `B` if `A` is a subtype of `B`.

    ⊢<: : ∀{Γ M A B}
      → Γ ⊢ M ⦂ A
    → A <: B
        -----------
      → Γ ⊢ M ⦂ B

In this chapter we study subtyping in the relatively simple context of
records and record types.  A *record* is a grouping of named values,
called *fields*. For example, one could represent a point on the
Cartesian plane with the following record.

    { x = 4, y = 1 }

A *record type* gives a type for each field. In the following, we
specify that the fields `x` and `y` both have type `ℕ`.

    { x : `ℕ,  y : `ℕ }

One record type is a subtype of another if it has all of the fields of
the supertype and if the types of those fields are subtypes of the
corresponding fields in the supertype. So, for example, a point in
three dimensions is a subtype of a point in two dimensions.

    { x : `ℕ,  y : `ℕ, z : `ℕ } <: { x : `ℕ,  y : `ℕ }

The elimination form for records is field access (aka. projection),
written `M # l`, and whose dynamic semantics is defined by the
following reduction rule, which says that accessing the field `lⱼ`
returns the value stored at that field.

    {l₁=v₁, ..., lⱼ=vⱼ, ..., lᵢ=vᵢ} # lⱼ —→  vⱼ

In this chapter we add records and record types to the simply typed
lambda calculus (STLC) and prove type safety. It is instructive to see
how the proof of type safety changes to handle subtyping.  Also, the
presence of subtyping makes the choice between extrinsic and intrinsic
typing more interesting by. If we wish to include the subsumption
rule, then we cannot use intrinsically typed terms, as intrinsic terms
only allow for syntax-directed rules, and subsumption is not syntax
directed.  A standard alternative to the subsumption rule is to
instead use subtyping in the typing rules for the elimination forms,
an approach called algorithmic typing. Here we choose to include the
subsumption rule and extrinsic typing, but we give an exercise at the
end of the chapter so the reader can explore algorithmic typing with
intrinsic terms.

## Syntax

The syntax includes that of the STLC with a few additions regarding
records that we explain in the following sections.

## Record Fields and their Properties

We represent field names as strings.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="Name"></a><a id="4606" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#4606" class="Function">Name</a> <a id="4611" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4613" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="4617" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#4606" class="Function">Name</a> <a id="4622" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4624" href="Agda.Builtin.String.html#206" class="Postulate">String</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
A record is traditionally written as follows

    { l₁ = M₁, ..., lᵢ = Mᵢ }

so a natural representation is a list of label-term pairs.
However, we find it more convenient to represent records as a pair of
vectors (Agda's `Vec` type), one vector of fields and one vector of terms:

    l₁, ..., lᵢ
    M₁, ..., Mᵢ

This representation has the advantage that the traditional subscript
notation `lᵢ` corresponds to indexing into a vector.

Likewise, a record type, traditionally written as

    { l₁ : A₁, ..., lᵢ : Aᵢ }

will be represented as a pair of vectors, one vector of fields and one
vector of types.

    l₁, ..., lᵢ
    A₁, ..., Aᵢ

The field names of a record type must be distinct, which we define as
follows.
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="distinct"></a><a id="5361" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5361" class="Function">distinct</a> <a id="5370" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5372" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="5374" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5374" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="5376" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5378" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="5381" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5383" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5383" class="Bound">n</a><a id="5384" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5386" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5388" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#935" class="Datatype">Vec</a> <a id="5392" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5374" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="5394" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5383" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="5396" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5398" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="5402" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5361" class="Function">distinct</a> <a id="5411" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#971" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a> <a id="5414" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5416" href="Agda.Builtin.Unit.html#137" class="Record">⊤</a>
<a id="5418" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5361" class="Function">distinct</a> <a id="5427" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5428" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5428" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="5430" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#990" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="5432" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5432" class="Bound">xs</a><a id="5434" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5436" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5438" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#535" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="5440" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5441" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5428" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="5443" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Membership.Setoid.html#824" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5445" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5432" class="Bound">xs</a><a id="5447" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5449" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Product.html#1162" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="5451" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5361" class="Function">distinct</a> <a id="5460" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5432" class="Bound">xs</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
For vectors of distinct elements, lookup is injective.

   <a id="5588" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5590" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5361" class="Function">distinct</a> <a id="5599" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5555" class="Bound">ls</a>  <a id="5603" class="Symbol">→</a>  <a id="5606" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#1491" class="Function">lookup</a> <a id="5613" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5555" class="Bound">ls</a> <a id="5616" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5572" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="5618" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#125" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="5620" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#1491" class="Function">lookup</a> <a id="5627" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5555" class="Bound">ls</a> <a id="5630" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5574" class="Bound">j</a>
   <a id="5635" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5637" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5572" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="5639" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#125" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="5641" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5574" class="Bound">j</a>

    <a id="6004" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#1090" class="Function">cong</a> <a id="6009" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Fin.Base.html#1053" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="6013" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6014" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5527" class="Function">distinct-lookup-inj</a> <a id="6034" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5987" class="Bound">dls</a> <a id="6038" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5993" class="Bound">lsij</a><a id="6042" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
We shall need to convert from an irrelevant proof of distinctness to a
relevant one. In general, the laundering of irrelevant proofs into
relevant ones is easy to do when the predicate in question is
decidable. The following is a decision procedure for whether a vector
is distinct.
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="distinct?"></a><a id="6336" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6336" class="Function">distinct?</a> <a id="6346" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6348" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="6350" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6350" class="Bound">n</a><a id="6351" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6353" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6355" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6356" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6356" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="6359" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6361" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#935" class="Datatype">Vec</a> <a id="6365" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#4606" class="Function">Name</a> <a id="6370" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6350" class="Bound">n</a><a id="6371" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6373" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6375" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#605" class="Datatype">Dec</a> <a id="6379" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6380" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5361" class="Function">distinct</a> <a id="6389" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6356" class="Bound">xs</a><a id="6391" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="6393" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6336" class="Function">distinct?</a> <a id="6403" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#971" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a> <a id="6406" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6408" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#641" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a> <a id="6412" href="Agda.Builtin.Unit.html#174" class="InductiveConstructor">tt</a>
<a id="6415" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6336" class="Function">distinct?</a> <a id="6425" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6426" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6426" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6428" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#990" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="6430" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6430" class="Bound">xs</a><a id="6432" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="6438" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="6443" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6426" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6445" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Membership.DecSetoid.html#834" class="Function Operator">∈?</a> <a id="6448" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6430" class="Bound">xs</a>
<a id="6451" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="6455" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="6457" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#641" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a> <a id="6461" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6461" class="Bound">x∈xs</a> <a id="6466" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6468" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#668" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a> <a id="6471" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="6473" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6473" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="6475" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6477" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#225" class="Field">proj₁</a> <a id="6483" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6473" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="6485" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6461" class="Bound">x∈xs</a>
<a id="6490" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="6494" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="6496" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#668" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a> <a id="6499" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6499" class="Bound">x∉xs</a>
    <a id="6509" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="6514" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6336" class="Function">distinct?</a> <a id="6524" class="Bound">xs</a>
<a id="6527" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="6531" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="6533" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#641" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a> <a id="6537" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6537" class="Bound">dxs</a> <a id="6541" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6543" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#641" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a> <a id="6547" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="6549" class="Bound">x∉xs</a> <a id="6555" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="6557" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6537" class="Bound">dxs</a> <a id="6561" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
<a id="6563" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="6567" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="6569" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#668" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a> <a id="6572" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6572" class="Bound">¬dxs</a> <a id="6577" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6579" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#668" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a> <a id="6582" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="6584" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6584" class="Bound">x₁</a> <a id="6587" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6589" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6572" class="Bound">¬dxs</a> <a id="6594" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6595" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#237" class="Field">proj₂</a> <a id="6601" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6584" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="6603" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
With this decision procedure in hand, we define the following
function for laundering irrelevant proofs of distinctness into
relevant ones.
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="distinct-relevant"></a><a id="6754" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6754" class="Function">distinct-relevant</a> <a id="6772" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6774" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="6776" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6777" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6777" class="Bound">n</a><a id="6778" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6780" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6780" class="Bound">fs</a> <a id="6783" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6785" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#935" class="Datatype">Vec</a> <a id="6789" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#4606" class="Function">Name</a> <a id="6794" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6777" class="Bound">n</a><a id="6795" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6797" class="Symbol">.(</a><a id="6799" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6799" class="Bound">d</a> <a id="6801" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6803" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5361" class="Function">distinct</a> <a id="6812" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6780" class="Bound">fs</a><a id="6814" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6816" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6818" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5361" class="Function">distinct</a> <a id="6827" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6780" class="Bound">fs</a>
<a id="6830" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6754" class="Function">distinct-relevant</a> <a id="6848" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6849" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6849" class="Bound">n</a><a id="6850" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6852" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6852" class="Bound">fs</a><a id="6854" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6856" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6856" class="Bound">d</a>
    <a id="6862" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="6867" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6336" class="Function">distinct?</a> <a id="6877" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6852" class="Bound">fs</a>
<a id="6880" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="6884" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="6886" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#641" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a> <a id="6890" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6890" class="Bound">dfs</a> <a id="6894" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6896" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6890" class="Bound">dfs</a>
<a id="6900" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="6904" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="6906" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#668" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a> <a id="6909" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6909" class="Bound">¬dfs</a> <a id="6914" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6916" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Empty.Irrelevant.html#327" class="Function">⊥-elimi</a> <a id="6924" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6925" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6909" class="Bound">¬dfs</a> <a id="6930" class="Bound">d</a><a id="6931" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
The fields of one record are a *subset* of the fields of another
record if every field of the first is also a field of the second.
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="_⊆_"></a><a id="7073" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#7073" class="Function Operator">_⊆_</a> <a id="7077" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7079" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="7081" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#7081" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="7083" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#7083" class="Bound">m</a><a id="7084" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7086" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7088" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#935" class="Datatype">Vec</a> <a id="7092" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#4606" class="Function">Name</a> <a id="7097" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#7081" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="7099" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7101" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#935" class="Datatype">Vec</a> <a id="7105" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#4606" class="Function">Name</a> <a id="7110" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#7083" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="7112" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7114" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="7118" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#7118" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="7121" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#7073" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="7123" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#7123" class="Bound">ys</a> <a id="7126" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7128" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7129" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#7129" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7131" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7133" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#4606" class="Function">Name</a><a id="7137" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7139" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7141" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#7129" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7143" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Membership.Setoid.html#824" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="7145" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#7118" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="7148" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7150" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#7129" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7152" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Membership.Setoid.html#824" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="7154" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#7123" class="Bound">ys</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
This subset relation is reflexive and transitive.
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="⊆-refl"></a><a id="7216" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#7216" class="Function">⊆-refl</a> <a id="7223" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7225" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="7227" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#7227" class="Bound">n</a><a id="7228" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7230" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#7230" class="Bound">ls</a> <a id="7233" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7235" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#935" class="Datatype">Vec</a> <a id="7239" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#4606" class="Function">Name</a> <a id="7244" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#7227" class="Bound">n</a><a id="7245" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7247" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7249" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#7230" class="Bound">ls</a> <a id="7252" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#7073" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="7254" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#7230" class="Bound">ls</a>

</pre>{% endraw %}
If `y` is an element of vector `xs`, then `y` is at some index `i` of
the vector.

If one vector `ns` is a subset of another `ms`, then for any element
`lookup ns i`, there is an equal element in `ms` at some index.
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="lookup-⊆"></a><a id="7960" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#7960" class="Function">lookup-⊆</a> <a id="7969"     <a id="8283" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#7960" class="Function">lookup-⊆</a> <a id="8292" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8293" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8240" class="Bound">n</a><a id="8294" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8296" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8297" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8244" class="Bound">m</a><a id="8298" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8300" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8301" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8252" class="Bound">ns</a><a id="8303" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8305" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8306" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8257" class="Bound">ms</a><a id="8308" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8310" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8311" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8266" class="Bound">i</a><a id="8312" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8314" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="8317" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8317" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8319" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8319" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="8321" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8323" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8269" class="Bound">x∷ns⊆ms</a> <a id="8331" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8317" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8333" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8334" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Relation.Unary.Any.html#1058" class="InductiveConstructor">there</a> <a id="8340" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8319" class="Bound">z</a><a id="8341" class="Symbol">))</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
## Types

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="8363" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Type"></a><a id="8368" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8368" class="Datatype">Type</a> <a id="8373" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8375" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="8379" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="Type._⇒_"></a><a id="8387" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8387" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_⇒_</a>   <a id="8393" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8395" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8368" class="Datatype">Type</a> <a id="8400" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8402" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8368" class="Datatype">Type</a> <a id="8407" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8409" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8368" class="Datatype">Type</a>
  <a id="Type.`ℕ"></a><a id="8416" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8416" class="InductiveConstructor">`ℕ</a>    <a id="8422" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8424" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8368" class="Datatype">Type</a>
  <a id="Type.｛_⦂_｝"></a><a id="8431" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8431" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">｛_⦂_｝</a> <a id="8437" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8439" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8440" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8440" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="8442" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8444" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#165" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="8445" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8447" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8448" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8448" class="Bound">ls</a> <a id="8451" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8453" class="Function">Name</a> <a id="8462" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8440" class="Bound">n</a><a id="8463" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8465" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8466" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8466" class="Bound">As</a> <a id="8469" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8471" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#935" class="Datatype">Vec</a> <a id="8475" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8368" class="Datatype">Type</a> <a id="8480" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8440" class="Bound">n</a><a id="8481" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8483" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8485" class="Symbol">.{</a><a id="8487" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8487" class="Bound">d</a> <a id="8489" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8491" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5361" class="Function">distinct</a> <a id="8500" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8448" class="Bound">ls</a><a id="8502" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8504" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8506" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8368" class="Datatype">Type</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
In addition to function types `A ⇒ B` and natural numbers `ℕ`, we
have the record type `｛ ls ⦂ As ｝`, where `ls` is a vector of field
names and `As` is a vector of types, as discussed above.  We require
that the field names be distinct, but we do not want the details of
the proof of distinctness to affect whether two record types are
equal, so we declare that parameter to be irrelevant by placing a `.`
in front of it.


## Subtyping

The subtyping relation, written `A <: B`, defines when an implicit
cast is allowed via the subsumption rule. The following data type
definition specifies the subtyping rules for natural numbers,
functions, and record types. We discuss each rule below.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="9211" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="_&lt;:_"></a><a id="9216" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9216" class="Datatype Operator">_&lt;:_</a> <a id="9221" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9223" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8368" class="Datatype">Type</a> <a id="9228" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9230" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8368" class="Datatype">Type</a> <a id="9235" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9237" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="9241" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="_&lt;:_.&lt;:-nat"></a><a id="9249" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9249" class="InductiveConstructor">&lt;:-nat</a> <a id="9256" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9258" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8416" class="InductiveConstructor">`ℕ</a> <a id="9261" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9216" class="Datatype Operator">&lt;:</a> <a id="9264" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8416" class="InductiveConstructor">`ℕ</a>

  <a id="_&lt;:_.&lt;:-fun"></a><a id="9270" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9270" class="InductiveConstructor">&lt;:-fun</a> <a id="9277" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9279" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="9281" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9281" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9283" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9283" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="9285" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9285" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="9287" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9287" class="Bound">D</a> <a id="9289" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9291" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8368" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="9295" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="9301" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9303" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9285" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="9305" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9216" class="Datatype Operator">&lt;:</a> <a id="9308" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9281" class="Bound">A</a>  <a id="9311" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9313" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9283" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="9315" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9216" class="Datatype Operator">&lt;:</a> <a id="9318" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9287" class="Bound">D</a>

    <a id="9347" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9349" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9281" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9351" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8387" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="9353" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9283" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="9355" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9216" class="Datatype Operator">&lt;:</a> <a id="9358" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9285" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="9360" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8387" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="9362" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9287" class="Bound">D</a>

  <a id="_&lt;:_.&lt;:-rcd"></a><a id="9367" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9367" class="InductiveConstructor">&lt;:-rcd</a> <a id="9374" class="Symbol">:</a>  <a id="9377" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="9379" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9379" class="Bound">m</a><a id="9380" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9382" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9382" class="Bound">ks</a> <a id="9385" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9387" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#935" class="Datatype">Vec</a> <a id="9391" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#4606" class="Function">Name</a> <a id="9396" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9379" class="Bound">m</a><a id="9397" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9399" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9399" class="Bound">Ss</a> <a id="9402" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9404" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#935" class="Datatype">Vec</a> <a id="9408" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8368" class="Datatype">Type</a> <a id="9413" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9379" class="Bound">m</a><a id="9414" class="Symbol">}.{</a><a id="9417" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9417" class="Bound">d1</a> <a id="9420" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9422" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5361" class="Function">distinct</a> <a id="9431" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9382" class="Bound">ks</a><a id="9433" class="Symbol">}</a>

    <a id="9509" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9511" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9452" class="Bound">ls</a> <a id="9514" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#7073" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="9516" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9382" class="Bound">ks</a>
    <a id="9523" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9525" class="Symbol">(∀{</a><a id="9528" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9528" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="9530" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9532" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Fin.Base.html#1000" class="Datatype">Fin</a> <a id="9536" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9449" class="Bound">n</a><a id="9537" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9539" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9539" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="9541" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9543" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Fin.Base.html#1000" class="Datatype">Fin</a> <a id="9547" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9379" class="Bound">m</a><a id="9548" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9550" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9552" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#1491" class="Function">lookup</a> <a id="9559" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9382" class="Bound">ks</a> <a id="9562" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9539" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="9564" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#125" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="9566" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#1491" class="Function">lookup</a> <a id="9573" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9452" class="Bound">ls</a> <a id="9576" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9528" class="Bound">i</a>
                               <a id="9609" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9611" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#1491" class="Function">lookup</a> <a id="9618" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9399" class="Bound">Ss</a> <a id="9621" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9539" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="9623" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9216" class="Datatype Operator">&lt;:</a> <a id="9626" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#1491" class="Function">lookup</a> <a id="9633" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9469" class="Bound">Ts</a> <a id="9636" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9528" class="Bound">i</a><a id="9637" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="9645" class="Comment">------------------------------------------------------</a>
    <a id="9704" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9706" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8431" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">｛</a> <a id="9708" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9382" class="Bound">ks</a> <a id="9711" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8431" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⦂</a> <a id="9713" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9399" class="Bound">Ss</a> <a id="9716" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8431" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">｝</a> <a id="9718" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9719" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9417" class="Bound">d1</a><a id="9721" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9723" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9216" class="Datatype Operator">&lt;:</a> <a id="9726" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8431" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">｛</a> <a id="9728" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9452" class="Bound">ls</a> <a id="9731" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8431" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⦂</a> <a id="9733" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9469" class="Bound">Ts</a> <a id="9736" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8431" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">｝</a> <a id="9738" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9739" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9487" class="Bound">d2</a><a id="9741" class="Symbol">}</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
The rule `<:-nat` says that `ℕ` is a subtype of itself.

The rule `<:-fun` is the traditional rule for function types, which is
best understood with the below diagram. It answers the question, when
can a function of type `A ⇒ B` be used in place of a function of type
`C ⇒ D`. It will be called with an argument of type `C`, so we need to
convert from `C` to `A`. We then call the function to get the result
of type `B`. Finally, we need to convert from `B` to `D`. Note that
the direction of subtyping for the parameters is swapped (`C <: A`), a
phenomenon named contra-variance.

    C <: A
    ⇓    ⇓
    D :> B

The record subtyping rule (`<:-rcd`) characterizes when a record of
one type can safely be used in place of another record type.  The
first premise of the rule expresses _width subtyping_ by requiring
that all the field names in `ls` are also in `ks`. So it allows the
hiding of fields when going from a subtype to a supertype.
The second premise of the record subtyping rule (`<:-rcd`) expresses
_depth subtyping_, that is, it allows the types of the fields to
change according to subtyping. The following is an abbreviation for
this premise.
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="_⦂_&lt;:_⦂_"></a><a id="10912" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#10912" class="Function Operator">_⦂_&lt;:_⦂_</a> <a ## Subtyping is Reflexive

In this section we prove that subtyping is reflexive, that is, `A <:
A` for any type `A`. The proof does not go by induction on the type
`A` because of the `<:-rcd` rule. We instead use induction on the size
of the type. So we first define size of a type, and the size of a
vector of types, as follows.
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="ty-size"></a><a id="11447" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#11447" class="Function">ty-size</a> <a id="11455" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11457" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11458" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#11458" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="11460" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11462" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8368" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="11466" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11468" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11470" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#165" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>
<a id="vec-ty-size"></a><a id="11472" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#11472" class="Function">vec-ty-size</a> <a id="11484" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11486" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="11488" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11489" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#11489" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="11491" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11493" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#165" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="11494" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11496" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11498" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11499" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#11499" class="Bound">As</a> <a id="11502" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11504" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#935" class="Datatype">Vec</a> <a id="11508" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8368" class="Datatype">Type</a> <a id="11513" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#11489" class="Bound">n</a><a id="11514" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11516" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11518" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#165" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>

<a id="11521" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#11447" class="Function">ty-size</a> <a id="11529" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11530" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#11530" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="11532" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8387" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="11534" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#11534" class="Bound">B</a><a id="11535" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11537" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11539" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#196" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="11543" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11544" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#11447" class="Function">ty-size</a> <a id="11552" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#11530" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="11554" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#298" class="Primitive Operator">+</a> <a id="11556" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#11447" class="Function">ty-size</a> <a id="11564" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#11534" class="Bound">B</a><a id="11565" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>{% endraw %}
The size of a type is always positive.
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="ty-size-pos"></a><a id="11750" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#11750" class="Function">ty-size-pos</a> <a id="11762" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11764" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="11766" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11767" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#11767" class="Bound">A</a><a id="11768" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11770" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11772" class="Number">0</a> <a id="11774" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Nat.Base.html#1005" class="Function Operator">&lt;</a> <a id="11776" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#11447" class="Function">ty-size</a> <a id="11784" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#11767" class="Bound">A</a>
<a id="11786" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#11750" class="Function">ty-size-pos</a> <a id="11798" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11799" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#11799" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="11801" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8387" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="11803" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#11803" class="Bound">B</a><a id="11804" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11806" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11808" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Nat.Base.html#960" class="InductiveConstructor">s≤s</a> <a id="11812" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Nat.Base.html#918" class="InductiveConstructor">z≤n</a>

</pre>{% endraw %}
The size of a type in a vector is less-or-equal in size to the entire vector.
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="lookup-vec-ty-size"></a><a id="11967" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#11967" class="Function">lookup-vec-ty-size</a> <a id="11986" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11988" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="11990" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#11990" class="Bound">k</a><a id="11991" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11993" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11994" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#11994" class="Bound">As</a> <a id="11997" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11999" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#935" class="Datatype">Vec</a> <a id="12003" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8368" class="Datatype">Type</a> <a id="12008" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#11990" class="Bound">k</a><a id="12009" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12011" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12012" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12012" class="Bound">j</a><a id="12013" class="Symbol">}</a>
   <a id="12018" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12020" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#11447" class="Function">ty-size</a> <a id="12028" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12029" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#1491" class="Function">lookup</a> <a id="12036" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#11994" class="Bound">As</a> <a id="12039" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12012" class="Bound">j</a><a id="12040" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12042" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Nat.Base.html#895" class="Datatype Operator">≤</a> <a id="12044" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#11472" class="Function">vec-ty-size</a> <a id="12056" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#11994" class="Bound">As</a>

Here is the proof of reflexivity, by induction on the size of the type.
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="&lt;:-refl-aux"></a><a id="12291" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12291" class="Function">&lt;:-refl-aux</a> <a id="12303" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12305" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="12307" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12307" class="Bound">n</a><a id="12308" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="12310" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12310" class="Bound">A</a><a id="12311" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="12313" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12313" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="12315" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12317" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#11447" class="Function">ty-size</a> <a id="12325" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12310" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="12327" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Nat.Base.html#895" class="Datatype Operator">≤</a> <a id="12329" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12307" class="Bound">n</a><a id="12330" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12332" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12334" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12310" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="12336" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9216" class="Datatype Operator">&lt;:</a> <a id="12339" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12310" class="Bound">A</a>
<a id="12341" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12291" class="Function">&lt;:-refl-aux</a> <a id="12353" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12354" class="Number">0</a><a id="12355" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="12357" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12357" class="Bound">A</a><a id="12358" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="12360" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12360" class="Bound">m</a><a id="12361" class="Symbol">}</a>

    <a id="12420" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="12425" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12394" class="Bound">pos</a>

  <a id="12568" class="Keyword">let</a> <a id="12572" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12572" class="Bound">B&lt;:B</a> <a id="12577" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12579" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12291" class="Function">&lt;:-refl-aux</a> <a id="12591" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12592" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12491" class="Bound">n</a><a id="12593" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="12595" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12498" class="Bound">B</a><a id="12596" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="12598" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Nat.Properties.html#15250" class="Function">m+n≤o⇒n≤o</a> <a id="12608" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="12610" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12611" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Nat.Properties.html#3355" class="Function">≤-pred</a> <a id="12618" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12501" class="Bound">m</a><a id="12619" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12621" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12623" class="Keyword">in</a>

class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="12704" class="Argument">d2</a> <a id="12707" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12709" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12678" class="Bound">d</a><a id="12710" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12712" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#7216" class="Function">⊆-refl</a> <a id="12719" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12735" class="Function">G</a>
    <a id="12725" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="12735" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12735" class="Function">G</a> <a id="12737" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12739" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12667" class="Bound">ls</a> <a id="12742" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#10912" class="Function Operator">⦂</a> <a id="12744" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12672" class="Bound">As</a> <a id="12747" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#10912" class="Function Operator">&lt;:</a> <a id="12750" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12667" class="Bound">ls</a> <a id="12753" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#10912" class="Function Operator">⦂</a> <a id="12755" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12672" class="Bound">As</a>
    <a id="12762" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12735" class="Function">G</a> <a id="12764" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12765" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12765" class="Bound">i</a><a id="12766" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="12768" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12768" class="Bound">j</a><a id="12769" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12771" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12771" class="Bound">lij</a> <a id="12775" class="Keyword">rewrite</a> <a id="12783" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5527" class="Function">distinct-lookup-inj</a> <a id="12803" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12804" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6754" class="Function">distinct-relevant</a> <a id="12822" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12678" class="Bound">d</a><a id="12823" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12825" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12771" class="Bound">lij</a> <a id="12829" class="Symbol">=</a>
        <a id="12839" class="Keyword">let</a> <a id="12843" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12843" class="Bound">As[i]≤n</a> <a id="12851" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12853" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Nat.Properties.html#3815" class="Function">≤-trans</a> <a id="12861" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12862" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#11967" class="Function">lookup-vec-ty-size</a> <a id="12881" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12882" class="Argument">As</a> <a id="12885" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12887" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12672" class="Bound">As</a><a id="12889" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="12891" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12765" class="Bound">i</a><a id="12892" class="Symbol">})</a> <a id="12895" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12896" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Nat.Properties.html#3355" class="Function">≤-pred</a> <a id="12903" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12683" class="Bound">m</a><a id="12904" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12906" class="Keyword">in</a>
        <a id="12917" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12291" class="Function">&lt;:-refl-aux</a> <a id="12929" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12930" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12662" class="Bound">n</a><a id="12931" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="12933" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#1491" class="Function">lookup</a> <a id="12940" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12672" class="Bound">As</a> <a id="12943" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12765" class="Bound">i</a><a id="12944" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="12946" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12843" class="Bound">As[i]≤n</a><a id="12953" class="Symbol">}</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}The theorem statement uses `n` as an upper bound on the size of the type `A`
and proceeds by induction on `n`.

* If it is `0`, then we have a contradiction because the size of a type is always positive.

* If it is `suc n`, we proceed by cases on the type `A`.

  * If it is `ℕ`, then we have `ℕ <: ℕ` by rule `<:-nat`.
  * If it is `A ⇒ B`, then by induction we have `A <: A` and `B <: B`.
    We conclude that `A ⇒ B <: A ⇒ B` by rule `<:-fun`.
  * If it is `｛ ls ⦂ As ｝`, then it suffices to prove that
    `ls ⊆ ls` and `ls ⦂ As <: ls ⦂ As`. The former is proved by `⊆-refl`.
    Regarding the latter, we need to show that for any `i` and `j`,
    `lookup ls j ≡ lookup ls i` implies `lookup As j <: lookup As i`.
    Because `lookup` is injective on distinct vectors, we have `i ≡ j`.
    We then use the induction hypothesis to show that
    `lookup As i <: lookup As i`, noting that the size of
    `lookup As i` is less-than-or-equal to the size of `As`, which
    is one smaller than the size of `｛ ls ⦂ As ｝`.

The following corollary packages up reflexivity for ease of use.
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="&lt;:-refl"></a><a id="14050" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14050" class="Function">&lt;:-refl</a> <a id="14058" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14060" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="14062" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14062" class="Bound">A</a><a id="14063" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14065" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14067" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14062" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14069" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9216" class="Datatype Operator">&lt;:</a> <a id="14072" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14062" class="Bound">A</a>
<a id="14074" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14050" class="Function">&lt;:-refl</a> <a id="14082" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14083" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14083" class="Bound">A</a><a id="14084" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14086" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14088" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#12291" class="Function">&lt;:-refl-aux</a> <a id="14100" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14101" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#11447" class="Function">ty-size</a> <a id="14109" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14083" class="Bound">A</a><a id="14110" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14112" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14083" class="Bound">A</a><a id="14113" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14115" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Nat.Properties.html#3632" class="Function">≤-refl</a><a id="14121" class="Symbol">}</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
## Subtyping is transitive

    <a id="14514" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14515" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9367" class="InductiveConstructor">&lt;:-rcd</a> <a id="14522" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14522" class="Bound">ms⊆ls</a> <a id="14528" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14528" class="Bound">As&lt;:Bs</a><a id="14534" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14536" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14537" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9367" class="InductiveConstructor">&lt;:-rcd</a> <a id="14544" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14544" class="Bound">ns⊆ms</a> <a id="14550" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14550" class="Bound">Bs&lt;:Cs</a><a id="14556" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14558" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="14564" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9367" class="InductiveConstructor">&lt;:-rcd</a> <a id="14571" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14572" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#7291" class="Function">⊆-trans</a> <a id="14580" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14544" class="Bound">ns⊆ms</a> <a id="14586" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14522" class="Bound">ms⊆ls</a><a id="14591" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14593" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14614" class="Function">As&lt;:Cs</a>
    <a id="14604" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="14614" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14614" class="Function">As&lt;:Cs</a> <a id="14621" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14623" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14454" class="Bound">ls</a> <a id="14626" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#10912" class="Function Operator">⦂</a> <a id="14628" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14459" class="Bound">As</a> <a id="14631" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#10912" class="Function Operator">&lt;:</a> <a id="14634" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14493" class="Bound">ns</a> <a id="14637" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#10912" class="Function Operator">⦂</a> <a id="14639" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14498" class="Bound">Cs</a>
    <a id="14646" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14614" class="Function">As&lt;:Cs</a> <a id="14653" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14654" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14654" class="Bound">i</a><a id="14655" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14657" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14657" class="Bound">j</a><a id="14658" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14660" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14660" class="Bound">ls[j]=ns[i]</a>
        <a id="14680" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="14685" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#7960" class="Function">lookup-⊆</a> <a id="14694" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14695" class="Argument">i</a> <a id="14697" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14699" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14654" class="Bound">i</a><a id="14700" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14702" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14544" class="Bound">ns⊆ms</a>
    <a id="14712" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="14716" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="14718" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="14720" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14720" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="14722" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="14724" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14724" class="Bound">ns[i]=ms[k]</a> <a id="14736" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="14738" class="Symbol">=</a>
        <a id="14748" class="Keyword">let</a> <a id="14752" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14752" class="Bound">As[j]&lt;:Bs[k]</a> <a id="14765" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14767" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14528" class="Bound">As&lt;:Bs</a> <a id="14774" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14775" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14720" class="Bound">k</a><a id="14776" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14778" class="Bound">j</a><a id="14779" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14781" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14782" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#984" class="Function">trans</a> <a id="14788" class="Bound">ls[j]=ns[i]</a> <a id="14800" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14724" class="Bound">ns[i]=ms[k]</a><a id="14811" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14813" class="Keyword">in</a>
        <a id="14824" class="Keyword">let</a> <a id="14828" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14828" class="Bound">Bs[k]&lt;:Cs[i]</a> <a id="14841" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14843" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14550" class="Bound">Bs&lt;:Cs</a> <a id="14850" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14851" class="Bound">i</a><a id="14852" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14854" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14720" class="Bound">k</a><a id="14855" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14857" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14858" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#939" class="Function">sym</a> <a id="14862" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14724" class="Bound">ns[i]=ms[k]</a><a id="14873" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14875" class="Keyword">in</a>
        <a id="14886" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14160" class="Function">&lt;:-trans</a> <a id="14895" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14752" class="Bound">As[j]&lt;:Bs[k]</a> <a id="14908" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14828" class="Bound">Bs[k]&lt;:Cs[i]</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
The proof is by induction on the derivations of `A <: B` and `B <: C`.

* If both derivations end with `<:-nat`: then we immediately conclude that `ℕ <: ℕ`.

* If both derivations end with `<:-fun`:
  we have `A₁ ⇒ A₂ <: B₁ ⇒ B₂` and  `B₁ ⇒ B₂ <: C₁ ⇒ C₂`.
  So `A₁ <: B₁` and `B₁ <: C₁`, thus `A₁ <: C₁` by the induction hypothesis.
  We also have `A₂ <: B₂` and `B₂ <: C₂`, so by the induction hypothesis
  we have `A₂ <: C₂`. We conclude that `A₁ ⇒ A₂ <: C₁ ⇒ C₂` by rule `<:-fun`.

* If both derivations end with `<:-rcd`, so we have
  `｛ ls ⦂ As ｝ <: ｛ ms ⦂ Bs ｝` and `｛ ms ⦂ Bs ｝ <: ｛ ns ⦂ Cs ｝`.
  From `ls ⊆ ms` and `ms ⊆ ns` we have `ls ⊆ ns` because `⊆` is transitive.
  Next we need to prove that `ls ⦂ As <: ns ⦂ Cs`.
  Suppose `lookup ls j ≡ lookup ns i` for an arbitrary `i` and `j`.
  We need to prove that `lookup As j <: lookup Cs i`.
  By the induction hypothesis, it suffices to show
  that `lookup As j <: lookup Bs k` and `lookup Bs k <: lookup Cs i` for some `k`.
  We can obtain the former from `｛ ls ⦂ As ｝ <: ｛ ms ⦂ Bs ｝`
  if we can prove that `lookup ls j ≡ lookup ms k`.
  We already have `lookup ls j ≡ lookup ns i` and we
  obtain `lookup ns i ≡ lookup ms k` by use of the lemma `lookup-⊆`,
  noting that `ns ⊆ ms`.
  We can obtain the later, that `lookup Bs k <: lookup Cs i`,
  from `｛ ms ⦂ Bs ｝ <: ｛ ns ⦂ Cs ｝`.
  It suffices to show that `lookup ms k ≡ lookup ns i`,
  which we have by symmetry.


## Contexts

We choose to represent variables with de Bruijn indices, so contexts
are sequences of types.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="16469" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Context"></a><a id="16474" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16474" class="Datatype">Context</a> <a id="16482" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16484" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="16488" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="Context.∅"></a><a id="16496" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16496" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a>   <a id="16500" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16502" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16474" class="Datatype">Context</a>
  <a id="Context._,_"></a><a id="16512" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16512" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a> <a id="16516" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16518" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16474" class="Datatype">Context</a> <a id="16526" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16528" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8368" class="Datatype">Type</a> <a id="16533" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16535" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16474" class="Datatype">Context</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
## Variables and the lookup judgment

The lookup judgment is a three-place relation, with a context, a de
Bruijn index, and a type.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="16685" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="_∋_⦂_"></a><a id="16690" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16690" class="Datatype Operator">_∋_⦂_</a> <a id="16696" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16698" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16474" class="Datatype">Context</a> <a id="16706" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16708" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#165" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="16710" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16712" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8368" class="Datatype">Type</a> <a id="16717" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16719" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="16723" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="_∋_⦂_.Z"></a><a id="16732" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16732" class="InductiveConstructor">Z</a> <a id="16734" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16736" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="16738" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16739" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16739" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="16741" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16741" class="Bound">A</a><a id="16742" class="Symbol">}</a>
      <a id="16750" class="Comment">------------------</a>
    <a id="16773" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16775" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16739" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="16777" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16512" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="16779" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16741" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="16781" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16690" class="Datatype Operator">∋</a> <a id="16783" class="Number">0</a> <a id="16785" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16690" class="Datatype Operator">⦂</a> <a id="16787" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16741" class="Bound">A</a>
