    <a id="16812" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16814" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16799" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="16816" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16690" class="Datatype Operator">∋</a> <a id="16818" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16801" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="16820" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16690" class="Datatype Operator">⦂</a> <a id="16822" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16803" class="Bound">A</a>
      <a id="16830" class="Comment">------------------</a>
    <a id="16853" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16855" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16799" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="16857" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16512" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="16859" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16805" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="16861" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16690" class="Datatype Operator">∋</a> <a id="16863" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16864" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#196" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="16868" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16801" class="Bound">x</a><a id="16869" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16871" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16690" class="Datatype Operator">⦂</a> <a id="16873" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16803" class="Bound">A</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
* The index `0` has the type at the front of the context.

* For the index `suc x`, we recursively look up its type in the
  remaining context `Γ`.


## Terms and the typing judgment

As mentioned above, variables are de Bruijn indices, which we
represent with natural numbers.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="Id"></a><a id="17163" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17163" class="Function">Id</a> <a id="17166" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17168" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="17172" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17163" class="Function">Id</a> <a id="17175" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17177" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#165" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
Our terms are extrinsic, so we define a `Term` data type similar to
the one in the [Lambda]({{ site.baseurl }}/Lambda/) chapter, but adapted for de
Bruijn indices.  The two new term constructors are for record creation
and field access.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="17426" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Term"></a><a id="17431" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17431" class="Datatype">Term</a> <a id="17436" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17438" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="17442" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="Term.`_"></a><a id="17450" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17450" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`_</a>                      <a id="17474" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17476" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17163" class="Function">Id</a> <a id="17479" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17481" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17431" class="Datatype">Term</a>
  <a id="Term.ƛ_"></a><a id="17488" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17488" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ_</a>                      <a id="17512" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17514" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17431" class="Datatype">Term</a> <a id="17519" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17521" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17431" class="Datatype">Term</a>
  <a id="Term._·_"></a><a id="17528" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17528" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_·_</a>                     <a id="17552" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17554" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17431" class="Datatype">Term</a> <a id="17559" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17561" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17431" class="Datatype">Term</a> <a id="17566" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17568" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17431" class="Datatype">Term</a>
  <a id="Term.`zero"></a><a id="17575" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17575" class="InductiveConstructor">`zero</a>                   <a id="17599" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17601" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17431" class="Datatype">Term</a>
  <a id="Term.`suc_"></a><a id="17608" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17608" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`suc_</a>                   <a id="17632" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17634" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17431" class="Datatype">Term</a> <a id="17639" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17641" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17431" class="Datatype">Term</a>

  <a id="Term._#_"></a><a id="17820" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17820" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_#_</a>                     <a id="17844" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17846" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17431" class="Datatype">Term</a> <a id="17851" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17853" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#4606" class="Function">Name</a> <a id="17858" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17860" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17431" class="Datatype">Term</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
In a record `｛ ls := Ms ｝`, we refer to the vector of terms `Ms` as
the *field initializers*.

The typing judgment takes the form `Γ ⊢ M ⦂ A` and relies on an
auxiliary judgment `Γ ⊢* Ms ⦂ As` for typing a vector of terms.

     <a id="19361" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19363" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#19314" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="19365" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#18166" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="19367" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#19316" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="19369" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#18166" class="Datatype Operator">⦂</a> <a id="19371" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#19336" class="Bound">A</a>

     <a id="19398" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19400" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#19314" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="19402" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#18103" class="Datatype Operator">⊢*</a> <a id="19405" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19406" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#19316" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="19408" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#990" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="19410" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#19319" class="Bound">Ms</a><a id="19412" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19414" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#18103" class="Datatype Operator">⦂</a> <a id="19416" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19417" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#19336" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="19419" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#990" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="19421" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#19339" class="Bound">As</a><a id="19423" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
Most of the typing rules are adapted from those in the [Lambda]({{ site.baseurl }}/Lambda/)
chapter. Here we discuss the three new rules.

* Rule `⊢rcd`: A record is well-typed if the field initializers `Ms`
  have types `As`, to match the record type. Also, the vector of field
  names is required to be distinct.

* Rule `⊢#`: A field access is well-typed if the term `M` has record type,
  the field `l` is at some index `i` in the record type's vector of field names,
  and the result type `A` is at index `i` in the vector of field types.

* Rule `⊢<:`: (Subsumption) If a term `M` has type `A`, and `A <: B`,
  then term `M` also has type `B`.


## Renaming and Substitution

In preparation of defining the reduction rules for this language, we
define simultaneous substitution using the same recipe as in the
[DeBruijn]({{ site.baseurl }}/DeBruijn/) chapter, but adapted to extrinsic
terms. Thus, the `subst` function is split into two parts: a raw
`subst` function that operators on terms and a `subst-pres` lemma that
proves that substitution preserves types. We define `subst` in this
section and postpone `subst-pres` to the
[Preservation](#subtyping-preservation) section.  Likewise for `rename`.

We begin by defining the `ext` function on renamings.
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="ext"></a><a id="20698" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#20698" class="Function">ext</a> <a id="20702" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20704" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20705" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17163" class="Function">Id</a> <a id="20708" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20710" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17163" class="Function">Id</a><a id="20712" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20714" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20716" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20717" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17163" class="Function">Id</a> <a id="20720" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20722" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17163" class="Function">Id</a><a id="20724" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="20726" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#20698" class="Function">ext</a> <a id="20730" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#20730" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="20732" class="Number">0</a>      <a id="20739" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="20742" class="Number">0</a>
<a id="20744" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#20698" class="Function">ext</a> <a id="20748" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#20748" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="20750" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20751" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#196" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="20755" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#20755" class="Bound">x</a><a id="20756" class="Symbol">)</a>  <a id="20759" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="20762" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#196" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="20766" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20767" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#20748" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="20769" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#20755" class="Bound">x</a><a id="20770" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
The `rename` function is defined mutually with the auxiliary
`rename-vec` function, which is needed in the case for records.
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="rename-vec"></a><a id="20906" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#20906" class="Function">rename-vec</a> <a id="20917" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20919" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20920" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17163" class="Function">Id</a> <a id="20923" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20925" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17163" class="Function">Id</a><a id="20927" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20929" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20931" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="20933" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#20933" class="Bound">n</a><a id="20934" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20936" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20938" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#935" class="Datatype">Vec</a> <a id="20942" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17431" class="Datatype">Term</a> <a id="20947" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#20933" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="20949" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20951" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#935" class="Datatype">Vec</a> <a id="20955" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17431" class="Datatype">Term</a> <a id="20960" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#20933" class="Bound">n</a>

With the `rename` function in hand, we can define the `exts` function
on substitutions.

</pre>{% endraw %}
We define `subst` mutually with the auxiliary `subst-vec` function,
which is needed in the case for records.

As usual, we implement single substitution using simultaneous
substitution.

## Values

We extend the definition of `Value` to include a clause for records.
In a call-by-value language, a record is usually only considered a
value if all its field initializers are values. Here we instead treat
records in a lazy fashion, declaring any record to be a value, to save
on some extra bookkeeping.

## Reduction

The following datatype `_—→_` defines the reduction relation for the
STLC with records. We discuss the two new rules for records in the
following paragraph.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="23486" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="_—→_"></a><a id="23491" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#23491" class="Datatype Operator">_—→_</a> <a id="23496" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23498" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17431" class="Datatype">Term</a> <a id="23503" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23505" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17431" class="Datatype">Term</a> <a id="23510" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23512" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="23516" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="_—→_.ξ-·₁"></a><a id="23525" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#23525" class="InductiveConstructor">ξ-·₁</a> <a id="23530" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23532" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="23534" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23535" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#23535" class="Bound">L</a> <a id="23537" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#23537" class="Bound">L′</a> <a id="23540" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#23540" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="23542" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23544" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17431" class="Datatype">Term</a><a id="23548" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="23554" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23556" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#23535" class="Bound">L</a> <a id="23558" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#23491" class="Datatype Operator">—→</a> <a id="23561" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#23537" class="Bound">L′</a>

<a id="24453" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="24455" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24456" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#24456" class="Bound">n</a><a %}#4606" class="Function">Name</a> <a id="24473" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#24456" class="Bound">n</a><a id="24474" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="24476" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#24476" class="Bound">Ms</a> <a id="24479" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24481" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#935" class="Datatype">Vec</a> <a id="24485" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17431" class="Datatype">Term</a> <a id="24490" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#24456" class="Bound">n</a><a id="24491" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24493" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24494" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#24494" class="Bound">l</a><a id="24495" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="24497" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Fin.Base.html#1000" class="Datatype">Fin</a> <a id="24505" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#24456" class="Bound">n</a><a id="24506" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="24512" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24514" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#1491" class="Function">lookup</a> <a id="24521" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#24459" class="Bound">ls</a> <a id="24524" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#24497" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="24526" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#125" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="24528" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#24494" class="Bound">l</a>
      <a id="24536" class="Comment">---------------------------------</a>
    <a id="24574" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24576" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17742" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">｛</a> <a id="24578" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#24459" class="Bound">ls</a> <a id="24581" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17742" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">:=</a> <a id="24584" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#24476" class="Bound">Ms</a> <a id="24587" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17742" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">｝</a> <a id="24589" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17820" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">#</a> <a id="24591" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#24494" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="24593" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#23491" class="Datatype Operator">—→</a>  <a id="24597" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#1491" class="Function">lookup</a> <a id="24604" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#24476" class="Bound">Ms</a> <a id="24607" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#24497" class="Bound">j</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
We have just two new reduction rules:
* Rule `ξ-#`: A field access expression `M # l` reduces to `M′ # l`
   provided that `M` reduces to `M′`.

* Rule `β-#`: When field access is applied to a record,
   and if the label `l` is at position `j` in the vector of field names,
   then result is the term at position `j` in the field initializers.


## Canonical Forms

As in the [Properties]({{ site.baseurl }}/Properties/) chapter, we
define a `Canonical V ⦂ A` relation that characterizes the well-typed
values.  The presence of the subsumption rule impacts its definition
because we must allow the type of the value `V` to be a subtype of `A`.

</pre>{% endraw %}
Every closed, well-typed value is canonical:

<a id="26501" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#25856" class="Function">canonical</a> <a id="26511" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="26512" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#19162" class="InductiveConstructor">⊢&lt;:</a> <a id="26516" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#26516" class="Bound">⊢V</a> <a id="26519" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="26520" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9367" class="InductiveConstructor">&lt;:-rcd</a> <a id="26527" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="26528" class="Argument">ks</a> <a id="26531" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="26533" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#26533" class="Bound">ks</a><a id="26535" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="26537" class="Argument">ls</a> <a id="26540" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="26542" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#26542" class="Bound">ls</a><a id="26544" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="26546" class="Argument">d2</a> <a id="26549" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="26551" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#26551" class="Bound">dls</a><a id="26554" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="26556" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#26556" class="Bound">ls⊆ks</a> <a id="26562" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#26562" class="Bound">ls⦂Ss&lt;:ks⦂Ts</a><a id="26574" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="26577" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#26577" class="Bound">VV</a>
    <a id="26584" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="26589" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#25856" class="Function">canonical</a> <a id="26599" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#26516" class="Bound">⊢V</a> <a id="26602" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#26577" class="Bound">VV</a>
<a id="26605" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="26609" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="26611" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#25600" class="InductiveConstructor">C-rcd</a> <a id="26617" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="26618" class="Argument">ks</a> <a id="26621" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="26623" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#26623" class="Bound">ks′</a><a id="26626" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="26628" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#26628" class="Bound">⊢Ms</a> <a id="26632" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#26632" class="Bound">dks′</a> <a id="26637" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#26637" class="Bound">As&lt;:Ss</a> <a id="26644" class="Symbol">=</a>
      <a id="26652" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#25600" class="InductiveConstructor">C-rcd</a> <a id="26658" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="26659" class="Argument">dls</a> <a id="26663" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="26665" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6754" class="Function">distinct-relevant</a> <a id="26683" class="Bound">dls</a><a id="26686" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="26688" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#26628" class="Bound">⊢Ms</a> <a id="26692" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#26632" class="Bound">dks′</a> <a id="26697" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="26698" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#14160" class="Function">&lt;:-trans</a> <a id="26707" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#26637" class="Bound">As&lt;:Ss</a> <a id="26714" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="26715" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9367" class="InductiveConstructor">&lt;:-rcd</a> <a id="26722" class="Bound">ls⊆ks</a> <a id="26728" class="Bound">ls⦂Ss&lt;:ks⦂Ts</a><a id="26740" class="Symbol">))</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}The case for subsumption (`⊢<:`) is interesting. We proceed by
cases on the derivation of subtyping.

* If the last rule is `<:-nat`, then we have `∅ ⊢ V ⦂ ℕ`
  and the induction hypothesis gives us `Canonical V ⦂ ℕ`.

* If the last rule is `<:-fun`, then we have `A ⇒ B <: C ⇒ D`
  and `∅ ⊢ ƛ N ⦂ A ⇒ B`. By the induction hypothesis,
  we have `∅ , A′ ⊢ N ⦂ B′` and `A′ ⇒ B′ <: A ⇒ B` for some `A′` and `B′`.
  We conclude that `Canonical (ƛ N) ⦂ C ⇒ D` by rule `C-ƛ` and the transitivity of subtyping.

* If the last rule is `<:-rcd`, then we have `｛ ls ⦂ Ss ｝ <: ｛ ks ⦂ Ts ｝`
  and `∅ ⊢ ｛ ks′ := Ms ｝ ⦂ ｛ ks ⦂ Ss ｝`. By the induction hypothesis,
  we have `∅ ⊢* Ms ⦂ As`, `distinct ks′`, and `｛ ks′ ⦂ As ｝ <: ｛ ks ⦂ Ss ｝`.
  We conclude that `Canonical ｛ ks′ := Ms ｝ ⦂ ｛ ks ⦂ Ts ｝`
  by rule `C-rcd` and the transitivity of subtyping.


If a term is canonical, then it is also a value.
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="value"></a><a id="27640" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#27640" class="Function">value</a> <a id="27646" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="27648" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="27650" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="27651" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#27651" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="27653" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#27653" class="Bound">A</a><a id="27654" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="27658" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="27660" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#25267" class="Datatype Operator">Canonical</a> <a id="27670" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#27651" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="27672" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#25267" class="Datatype Operator">⦂</a> <a id="27674" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#27653" class="Bound">A</a>
    <a id="27680" class="Comment">----------------</a>

A canonical value is a well-typed value.

## Progress <a name="subtyping-progress"></a>

The Progress theorem states that a well-typed term may either take a
reduction step or it is already a value. The proof of Progress is like
the one in the [Properties]({{ site.baseurl }}/Properties/); it
proceeds by induction on the typing derivation and most of the cases
remain the same. Below we discuss the new cases for records and
subsumption.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="28512" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Progress"></a><a id="28517" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#28517" class="Datatype">Progress</a> <a id="28526" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28527" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#28527" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="28529" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28531" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17431" class="Datatype">Term</a><a id="28535" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28537" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28539" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="28543" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="Progress.step"></a><a id="28552" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#28552" class="InductiveConstructor">step</a> <a id="28557" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28559" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="28561" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28562" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#28562" class="Bound">N</a><a id="28563" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="28569" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28571" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#28527" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="28573" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#23491" class="Datatype Operator">—→</a> <a id="28576" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#28562" class="Bound">N</a>
      <a id="28584" class="Comment">----------</a>
    <a id="28599" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28601" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#28517" class="Datatype">Progress</a> <a id="28610" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#28527" class="Bound">M</a>

  <a id="Progress.done"></a><a id="28615" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#28615" class="InductiveConstructor">done</a> <a id="28620" class="Symbol">:</a>

      <a id="28642" class="Comment">----------</a>
    <a id="28657" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28659" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#28517" class="Datatype">Progress</a> <a id="28668" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#28527" class="Bound">M</a>

<a id="29874" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="29878" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="29880" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#25600" class="InductiveConstructor">C-rcd</a> <a id="29886" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="29887" class="Argument">ks</a> <a id="29890" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="29892" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#29892" class="Bound">ms</a><a id="29894" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="29896" class="Argument">As</a> <a id="29899" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="29901" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#29901" class="Bound">Bs</a><a id="29903" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="29905" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#29905" class="Bound">⊢Ms</a> <a id="29909" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="29911" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29912" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#9367" class="InductiveConstructor">&lt;:-rcd</a> <a id="29919" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#29919" class="Bound">ls⊆ms</a> <a id="29925" class="Symbol">_)</a>
    <a id="29932" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="29937" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#7960" class="Function">lookup-⊆</a> <a id="29946" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="29947" class="Argument">i</a> <a id="29949" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="29951" class="Bound">i</a><a id="29952" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="29954" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#29919" class="Bound">ls⊆ms</a>

<a id="30059" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#28679" class="Function">progress</a> <a id="30068" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30069" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#18841" class="InductiveConstructor">⊢rcd</a> <a id="30074" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#30074" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="30076" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#30076" class="Bound">d</a><a id="30077" class="Symbol">)</a>                         <a id="30103" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="30106" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#28615" class="InductiveConstructor">done</a> <a id="30111" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#23233" class="InductiveConstructor">V-rcd</a>
<a id="30117" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#28679" class="Function">progress</a> <a id="30126" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30127" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#19162" class="InductiveConstructor">⊢&lt;:</a> <a id="30131" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="30132" class="Argument">A</a> <a id="30134" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="30136" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#30136" class="Bound">A</a><a id="30137" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="30139" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#30139" class="Bound">B</a><a id="30140" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="30142" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#30142" class="Bound">⊢M</a> <a id="30145" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#30145" class="Bound">A&lt;:B</a><a id="30149" class="Symbol">)</a>           <a id="30161" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="30164" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#28679" class="Function">progress</a> <a id="30173" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#30142" class="Bound">⊢M</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}* Case `⊢#`: We have `Γ ⊢ M ⦂ ｛ ls ⦂ As ｝`, `lookup ls i ≡ l`, and `lookup As i ≡ A`.
  By the induction hypothesis, either `M —→ M′` or `M` is a value. In the later case we
  conclude that `M # l —→ M′ # l` by rule `ξ-#`. On the other hand, if `M` is a value,
  we invoke the canonical forms lemma to show that `M` has the form `｛ ms := Ms ｝`
  where `∅ ⊢* Ms ⦂ Bs` and `ls ⊆ ms`. By lemma `lookup-⊆`, we have
  `lookup ls i ≡ lookup ms k` for some `k`. Thus, we have `lookup ms k ≡ l`
  and we conclude `｛ ms := Ms ｝ # l —→ lookup Ms k` by rule `β-#`.

* Case `⊢rcd`: we immediately characterize the record as a value.

* Case `⊢<:`: we invoke the induction hypothesis on sub-derivation of `Γ ⊢ M ⦂ A`.


## Preservation <a name="subtyping-preservation"></a>

In this section we prove that when a well-typed term takes a reduction
step, the result is another well-typed term with the same type.

As mentioned earlier, we need to prove that substitution preserve
types, which in turn requires that renaming preserves types.  The
proofs of these lemmas are adapted from the intrinsic versions of the
`ext`, `rename`, `exts`, and `subst` functions in the
[DeBruijn]({{ site.baseurl }}/DeBruijn/) chapter.

We define the following abbreviation for a *well-typed renaming* from Γ
to Δ, that is, a renaming that sends variables in Γ to variables in Δ
with the same type.
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="_⦂ᵣ_⇒_"></a><a id="31551" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#31551" class="Function Operator">_⦂ᵣ_⇒_</a> <a id="31558" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31560" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31561" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17163" class="Function">Id</a> <a id="31564" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="31566" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17163" class="Function">Id</a><a id="31568" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="31570" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="31572" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16474" class="Datatype">Context</a> <a id="31580" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="31582" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16474" class="Datatype">Context</a> <a id="31590" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="31592" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="31596" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#31596" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="31598" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link The `ext` function takes a well-typed renaming from Γ to Δ
and extends it to become a renaming from (Γ , B) to (Δ , B).

  <a id="31797" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="31799" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#31790" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="31801" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#31551" class="Function Operator">⦂ᵣ</a> <a id="31804" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#31786" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="31806" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#31551" class="Function Operator">⇒</a> <a id="31808" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#31788" class="Bound">Δ</a>

Next we prove that both `rename` and `rename-vec` preserve types.  We
use the `ext-pres` lemma in each of the cases with a variable binding: `⊢ƛ`,
`⊢μ`, and `⊢case`.
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="ren-vec-pres"></a><a id="32129" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#32129" class="Function">ren-vec-pres</a> <a id="32142" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="32144" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="32146" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="32147" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#32147" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="32149" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#32149" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="32151" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#32151" class="Bound">ρ</a><a id="32152" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="32154" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#32154" class="Bound">n</a><a id="32155" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="32157" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#32157" class="Bound">Ms</a> <a id="32160" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="32162" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#935" class="Datatype">Vec</a> <a id="32166" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17431" class="Datatype">Term</a> <a id="32171" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#32154" class="Bound">n</a><a id="32172" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="32174" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#32174" class="Bound">As</a> <a id="32177" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="32179" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#935" class="Datatype">Vec</a> <a id="32183" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#8368" class="Datatype">Type</a> <a id="32188" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#32154" class="Bound">n</a><a id="32189" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="32193" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="32195" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#32151" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="32197" href="{% endraw %}{{ A *well-typed substitution* from Γ to Δ sends variables in Γ to terms
of the same type in the context Δ.
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="_⦂_⇒_"></a><a id="33401" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#33401" class="Function Operator">_⦂_⇒_</a> <a id="33407" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33409" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33410" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17163" class="Function">Id</a> <a id="33413" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="33415" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#17431" class="Datatype">Term</a><a id="33419" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33421" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="33423" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16474" class="Datatype">Context</a> <a id="33431" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="33433" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16474" class="Datatype">Context</a> <a id="33441" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="33443" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="33447" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#33447" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="33449" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link class="Bound">A</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
The `exts` function sends well-typed substitutions from Γ to Δ to
well-typed substitutions from (Γ , B) to (Δ , B). In the case for `S`,
we note that `exts σ (suc x) ≡ rename sub (σ x)`, so we need to prove
`Δ , B ⊢ rename suc (σ x) ⦂ A`, which we obtain by the `rename-pres`
lemma.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="exts-pres"></a><a id="33796" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#33796" class="Function">exts-pres</a> <a id="33806" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33808" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="33810" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="33811" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#33811" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="33813" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#33813" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="33815" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#33815" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="33817" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#33817" class="Bound">B</a><a id="33818" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="33822" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="33824" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#33815" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="33826" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#33401" class="Function Operator">⦂</a> <a id="33828" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#33811" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="33830" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#33401" class="Function Operator">⇒</a> <a id="33832" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#33813" class="Bound">Δ</a>
    <a id="33838" class="Comment">--------------------------------</a>
  <a id="33873" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="33875" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#21630" class="Function">exts</a> <a id="33880" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#33815" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="33882" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#33401" class="Function Operator">⦂</a> <a id="33884" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33885" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#33811" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="33887" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16512" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="33889" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#33817" class="Bound">B</a><a id="33890" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33892" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#33401" class="Function Operator">⇒</a> <a id="33894" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33895" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#33813" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="33897" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16512" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="33899" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#33817" class="Bound">B</a><a id="33900" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="33902" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#33796" class="Function">exts-pres</a> <a id="33912" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="33913" class="Argument">σ</a> <a id="33915" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="33917" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#33917" class="Bound">σ</a><a id="33918" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="33920" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#33920" class="Bound">σ⦂</a> <a id="33923" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16732" class="InductiveConstructor">Z</a> <a id="33925" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="33927" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#18211" class="InductiveConstructor">⊢`</a> <a id="33930" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16732" class="InductiveConstructor">Z</a>
<a id="33932" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#33796" class="Function">exts-pres</a> <a id="33942" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="33943" class="Argument">σ</a> <a id="33945" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="33947" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#33947" class="Bound">σ</a><a id="33948" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="33950" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#33950" class="Bound">σ⦂</a> <a id="33953" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33954" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16792" class="InductiveConstructor">S</a> <a id="33956" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="33957" class="Argument">x</a> <a id="33959" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="33961" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#33961" class="Bound">x</a><a id="33962" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="33964" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#33964" class="Bound">∋x</a><a id="33966" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33968" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="33970" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#32254" class="Function">rename-pres</a> <a id="33982" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="33983" class="Argument">ρ</a> <a id="33985" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="33987" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#196" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a><a id="33990" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="33992" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16792" class="InductiveConstructor">S</a> <a id="33994" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33995" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#33950" class="Bound">σ⦂</a> <a id="33998" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#33964" class="Bound">∋x</a><a id="34000" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
Now we prove that both `subst` and `subst-vec` preserve types.  We use
the `exts-pres` lemma in each of the cases with a variable binding:
`⊢ƛ`, `⊢μ`, and `⊢case`.

</pre>{% endraw %}
The fact that single substitution preserves types is a corollary
of `subst-pres`.

We require just one last lemma before we get to the proof of preservation.
The following lemma establishes that field access preserves types.

         <a id="35900" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="35902" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16496" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a> <a id="35904" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#18103" class="Datatype Operator">⊢*</a> <a id="35907" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#35863" class="Bound">Ms</a> <a id="35910" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#18103" class="Datatype Operator">⦂</a> <a id="35912" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#35843" class="Bound">As</a>

<a id="35973" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#35825" class="Function">field-pres</a> <a id="35984" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="35985" class="Argument">i</a> <a id="35987" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="35989" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Fin.Base.html#1022" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a><a id="35993" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="35995" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35996" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#19301" class="InductiveConstructor">⊢*-∷</a> <a id="36001" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#36001" class="Bound">⊢M</a> <a id="36004" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#36004" class="Bound">⊢Ms</a><a id="36007" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="36009" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#182" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="36014" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="36016" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#36001" class="Bound">⊢M</a>
<a id="36019" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#35825" class="Function">field-pres</a> <a id="36030" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="36031" class="Argument">i</a> <a id="36033" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="36035" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Fin.Base.html#1053" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="36039" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#36039" class="Bound">i</a><a id="36040" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="36042" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="36043" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#19301" class="InductiveConstructor">⊢*-∷</a> <a id="36048" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#36048" class="Bound">⊢M</a> <a id="36051" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#36051" class="Bound">⊢Ms</a><a id="36054" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="36056" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#36056" class="Bound">As[i]=A</a> <a id="36064" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="36066" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#35825" class="Function">field-pres</a> <a id="36077" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#36051" class="Bound">⊢Ms</a> <a id="36081" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#36056" class="Bound">As[i]=A</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}The proof is by induction on the typing derivation.

* Case `⊢-*-[]`: This case yields a contradiction because `Fin 0` is uninhabitable.

* Case `⊢-*-∷`: So we have `∅ ⊢ M ⦂ B` and `∅ ⊢* Ms ⦂ As`. We proceed by cases on `i`.

    * If it is `0`, then lookup yields term `M` and `A ≡ B`, so we conclude that `∅ ⊢ M ⦂ A`.

    * If it is `suc i`, then we conclude by the induction hypothesis.


We conclude this chapter with the proof of preservation. We discuss
the cases particular to records and subtyping in the paragraph
following the Agda proof.
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="preserve"></a><a id="36647" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#36647" class="Function">preserve</a> <a id="36656" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="36658" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="36660" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="36661" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#36661" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="36663" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#36663" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="36665" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#36665" class="Bound">A</a><a id="36666" class="Symbol">}</a>

  <a id="36684" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="36686" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#36661" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="36688" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#23491" class="Datatype Operator">—→</a> <a id="36691" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#36663" class="Bound">N</a>
    <a id="36697" class="Comment">----------</a>
  <a id="36710" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="36712" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#16496" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a> <a id="36714" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#18166" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="36716" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#36663" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="36718" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#18166" class="Datatype Operator">⦂</a> <a id="36720" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#36665" class="Bound">A</a>

    <a id="38025" class="Keyword">let</a> <a id="38029" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#38029" class="Bound">Ms[k]⦂As[i]</a> <a id="38041" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="38043" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#19162" class="InductiveConstructor">⊢&lt;:</a> <a id="38047" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#37942" class="Bound">⊢Ms[k]⦂Bs[k]</a> <a id="38060" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="38061" class="Bound">Bs&lt;:As</a> <a id="38068" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="38069" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#939" class="Function">sym</a> <a id="38073" class="Bound">ls[i]=ks[k]</a><a id="38084" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="38087" class="Keyword">in</a>
    <a id="38094" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#38029" class="Bound">Ms[k]⦂As[i]</a>
<a id="38106" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#36647" class="Function">preserve</a> <a id="38115" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="38116" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#19162" class="InductiveConstructor">⊢&lt;:</a> <a id="38120" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#38120" class="Bound">⊢M</a> <a id="38123" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#38123" class="Bound">B&lt;:A</a><a id="38127" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="38129" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#38129" class="Bound">M—→N</a>                       <a id="38156" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="38159" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#19162" class="InductiveConstructor">⊢&lt;:</a> <a id="38163" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="38164" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#36647" class="Function">preserve</a> <a id="38173" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#38120" class="Bound">⊢M</a> <a id="38176" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#38129" class="Bound">M—→N</a><a id="38180" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="38182" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#38123" class="Bound">B&lt;:A</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}Recall that the proof is by induction on the derivation of `∅ ⊢ M ⦂ A`
with cases on `M —→ N`.

* Case `⊢#` and `ξ-#`: So `∅ ⊢ M ⦂ ｛ ls ⦂ As ｝`, `lookup ls i ≡ l`, `lookup As i ≡ A`,
  and `M —→ M′`. We apply the induction hypothesis to obtain `∅ ⊢ M′ ⦂ ｛ ls ⦂ As ｝`
  and then conclude by rule `⊢#`.

* Case `⊢#` and `β-#`. We have `∅ ⊢ ｛ ks := Ms ｝ ⦂ ｛ ls ⦂ As ｝`, `lookup ls i ≡ l`,
  `lookup As i ≡ A`, `lookup ks j ≡ l`, and `｛ ks := Ms ｝ # l —→ lookup Ms j`.
  By the canonical forms lemma, we have `∅ ⊢* Ms ⦂ Bs`, `ls ⊆ ks` and `ks ⦂ Bs <: ls ⦂ As`.
  By lemma `lookup-⊆` we have `lookup ls i ≡ lookup ks k` for some `k`.
  Also, we have `∅ ⊢ lookup Ms k ⦂ lookup Bs k` by lemma `field-pres`.
  Then because `ks ⦂ Bs <: ls ⦂ As` and `lookup ks k ≡ lookup ls i`, we have
  `lookup Bs k <: lookup As i`. So by rule `⊢<:` we have
  `∅ ⊢ lookup Ms k ⦂ lookup As i`.
  Finally, because `lookup` is injective and `lookup ks j ≡ lookup ks k`,
  we have `j ≡ k` and conclude that `∅ ⊢ lookup Ms j ⦂ lookup As i`.

* Case `⊢<:`. We have `∅ ⊢ M ⦂ B`, `B <: A`, and `M —→ N`. We apply the induction hypothesis
  to obtain `∅ ⊢ N ⦂ B` and then subsumption to conclude that `∅ ⊢ N ⦂ A`.


#### Exercise `intrinsic-records` (stretch)

Formulate the language of this chapter, STLC with records, using
intrinsically typed terms. This requires taking an algorithmic approach
to the type system, which means that there is no subsumption rule and
instead subtyping is used in the elimination rules. For example,
the rule for function application would be:

    _·_ : ∀ {Γ A B C}
      → Γ ⊢ A ⇒ B
      → Γ ⊢ C
      → C <: A
        -------
      → Γ ⊢ B

#### Exercise `type-check-records` (practice)

Write a recursive function whose input is a `Term` and whose output
is a typing derivation for that term, if one exists.

    type-check : (M : Term) → (Γ : Context) → Maybe (Σ[ A ∈ Type ] Γ ⊢ M ⦂ A)

#### Exercise `variants` (recommended)

Add variants to the language of this chapter and update the proofs of
progress and preservation. The variant type is a generalization of a
sum type, similar to the way the record type is a generalization of
product. The following summarizes the treatment of variants in the
book Types and Programming Languages. A variant type is traditionally
written:

    〈l₁:A₁, ..., lᵤ:Aᵤ〉

The term for introducing a variant is

    〈l=t〉

and the term for eliminating a variant is

    case L of 〈l₁=x₁〉 ⇒ M₁ | ... | 〈lᵤ=xᵤ〉 ⇒ Mᵤ

The typing rules for these terms are

    (T-Variant)
    Γ ⊢ Mⱼ : Aⱼ
    ---------------------------------
    Γ ⊢ 〈lⱼ=Mⱼ〉 : 〈l₁=A₁, ... , lᵤ=Aᵤ〉


    (T-Case)
    Γ ⊢ L : 〈l₁=A₁, ... , lᵤ=Aᵤ〉
    ∀ i ∈ 1..u,   Γ,xᵢ:Aᵢ ⊢ Mᵢ : B
    ---------------------------------------------------
    Γ ⊢ case L of 〈l₁=x₁〉 ⇒ M₁ | ... | 〈lᵤ=xᵤ〉 ⇒ Mᵤ  : B

The non-algorithmic subtyping rules for variants are

    (S-VariantWidth)
    ------------------------------------------------------------
    〈l₁=A₁, ..., lᵤ=Aᵤ〉   <:   〈l₁=A₁, ..., lᵤ=Aᵤ, ..., lᵤ₊ₓ=Aᵤ₊ₓ〉

    (S-VariantDepth)
    ∀ i ∈ 1..u,    Aᵢ <: Bᵢ
    ---------------------------------------------
    〈l₁=A₁, ..., lᵤ=Aᵤ〉   <:   〈l₁=B₁, ..., lᵤ=Bᵤ〉

    (S-VariantPerm)
    ∀i∈1..u, ∃j∈1..u, kⱼ = lᵢ and Aⱼ = Bᵢ
    ----------------------------------------------
    〈k₁=A₁, ..., kᵤ=Aᵤ〉   <:   〈l₁=B₁, ..., lᵤ=Bᵤ〉

Come up with an algorithmic subtyping rule for variant types.

#### Exercise `<:-alternative` (stretch)

Revise this formalization of records with subtyping (including proofs
of progress and preservation) to use the non-algorithmic subtyping
rules for Chapter 15 of Types and Programming Languages, which we list here:

    (S-RcdWidth)
    --------------------------------------------------------------
    { l₁:A₁, ..., lᵤ:Aᵤ, ..., lᵤ₊ₓ:Aᵤ₊ₓ } <: { l₁:A₁, ..., lᵤ:Aᵤ }

    (S-RcdDepth)
        ∀i∈1..u, Aᵢ <: Bᵢ
    ----------------------------------------------
    { l₁:A₁, ..., lᵤ:Aᵤ } <: { l₁:B₁, ..., lᵤ:Bᵤ }

    (S-RcdPerm)
    ∀i∈1..u, ∃j∈1..u, kⱼ = lᵢ and Aⱼ = Bᵢ
    ----------------------------------------------
    { k₁:A₁, ..., kᵤ:Aᵤ } <: { l₁:B₁, ..., lᵤ:Bᵤ }

You will most likely need to prove inversion lemmas for the subtype relation
of the form:

    If S <: T₁ ⇒ T₂, then S ≡ S₁ ⇒ S₂, T₁ <: S₁, and S₂ <: T₂, for some S₁, S₂.

    If S <: { lᵢ : Tᵢ | i ∈ 1..n }, then S ≡ { kⱼ : Sⱼ | j ∈ 1..m }
    and { lᵢ | i ∈ 1..n } ⊆ { kⱼ | j ∈ 1..m }
    and Sⱼ <: Tᵢ for every i and j such that lᵢ = kⱼ.

## References

* John C. Reynolds. Using Category Theory to Design Implicit
  Conversions and Generic Operators.
  In Semantics-Directed Compiler Generation, 1980.
  LNCS Volume 94.

* Luca Cardelli. A semantics of multiple inheritance.  In Semantics of
  Data Types, 1984. Springer.

* Barbara H. Liskov and Jeannette M. Wing.  A Behavioral Notion of
  Subtyping. In ACM Trans. Program. Lang. Syst.  Volume 16, 1994.

* Types and Programming Languages. Benjamin C. Pierce. The MIT Press. 2002.
